        echo "âœ… æ­å–œï¼æ‰€æœ‰è§†é¢‘çš„è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯éƒ½å·²è·å–ï¼Œæ— éœ€â€œè¡¥è´§â€ã€‚"
        break
    else
        echo "â„¹ï¸  ç¬¬ ${round} è½®ï¼šéœ€è¦ä¸º ${MISSING_COUNT} ä¸ªæ–°è§†é¢‘è·å–è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚"
        # --- STEP 3: åˆ†æ‰¹â€œç²¾å‡†è¡¥è´§â€ ---
        echo -e "\nSTEP 3 (ç¬¬ ${round}/${MAX_RETRY_ROUNDS} è½®): å¼€å§‹åˆ†æ‰¹â€œç²¾å‡†è¡¥è´§â€"
        echo "-------------------------------------------------------"
        BATCH_COUNTER=0
        &gt; "${INFO_FAILED_IDS_FILE}"
        while read -r VIDEO_ID; do
            ((BATCH_COUNTER++))
            echo "è¡¥è´§ä¸­(${BATCH_COUNTER}/${MISSING_COUNT}): æ­£åœ¨è·å–ID ${VIDEO_ID} çš„è¯¦ç»†ä¿¡æ¯..."
            
            VIDEO_INFO=$(yt-dlp --proxy "socks5://127.0.0.1:${PROXY_PORT}" --print "%(upload_date)s\t%(id)s\t%(title)s" --ignore-errors --retries 10 "https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=${VIDEO_ID}")
            
            if [ -n "$VIDEO_INFO" ]; then
                echo -e "${VIDEO_INFO}" &gt;&gt; "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}"
            else
                echo "âš ï¸  è·å–ID ${VIDEO_ID} å¤±è´¥ï¼Œå·²è®°å½•åˆ°å¤±è´¥æ¸…å•ã€‚"
                echo "${VIDEO_ID}" &gt;&gt; "${INFO_FAILED_IDS_FILE}"
            fi

            if (( BATCH_COUNTER % DETAILS_FETCH_BATCH_SIZE == 0 &amp;&amp; BATCH_COUNTER &lt; MISSING_COUNT )); then
                SLEEP_TIME=$(( (RANDOM % 46) + 15 ));
                echo "â³ å®Œæˆä¸€æ‰¹â€œè¡¥è´§â€ï¼Œä¸ºå®‰å…¨èµ·è§ï¼Œè‡ªåŠ¨å†·å´ ${SLEEP_TIME} ç§’..."
                sleep ${SLEEP_TIME}
            else
                sleep 1
            fi
        done &lt; "${MISSING_IDS_FILE}"
        echo "âœ… ç¬¬ ${round} è½®â€œè¡¥è´§â€å°è¯•å®Œæˆï¼"
    fi

# --- STEP 4: æœ€ç»ˆå®¡è®¡ä¸æ ‡è®° ---

echo "-------------------------------------------------------"
echo "ğŸ”„ æ­£åœ¨è¿›è¡Œæœ€ç»ˆå®¡è®¡..."

FINAL_MISSING_COUNT=$(wc -l &lt; "${MISSING_IDS_FILE}" | tr -d ' ')
FINAL_SUCCESS_COUNT=$(wc -l &lt; "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}" | tr -d ' ')
GOAL_COUNT=$(wc -l &lt; "${GOAL_IDS_FILE}" | tr -d ' ')

echo "ğŸ“Š ä¿¡æ¯é‡‡é›†æœ€ç»ˆå®¡è®¡æŠ¥å‘Šï¼š"
echo "    - æ€»ç›®æ ‡è§†é¢‘æ•°: ${GOAL_COUNT}"
echo "    - æˆåŠŸè·å–ä¿¡æ¯æ•°: ${FINAL_SUCCESS_COUNT}"
echo "    - æœ€ç»ˆç¼ºå¤±æ•°: ${FINAL_MISSING_COUNT}"

if [ "${FINAL_SUCCESS_COUNT}" -eq "${GOAL_COUNT}" ]; then
    echo "âœ… å®Œç¾ï¼æ‰€æœ‰è§†é¢‘ä¿¡æ¯å‡å·²æˆåŠŸè·å–ã€‚"
    echo "ğŸ”„ æ­£åœ¨å¯¹æœ€ç»ˆæ¸…å•è¿›è¡Œæ’åºï¼ˆä»æ—§åˆ°æ–°ï¼‰..."
    sort -k1,1 "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}" &gt; "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}.sorted"
    mv "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}.sorted" "${MASTER_METADATA_FILE}"
    touch "${METADATA_COMPLETE_FLAG}"
    echo "âœ… æ¸…å•å·²æ’åºå¹¶æ ‡è®°ä¸ºâ€œå·²å®Œæˆâ€ã€‚"
else
    echo "âŒ è­¦å‘Šï¼šç»è¿‡å¤šè½®å°è¯•ï¼Œä»æœ‰ ${FINAL_MISSING_COUNT} ä¸ªè§†é¢‘ä¿¡æ¯è·å–å¤±è´¥ã€‚"
    echo "    å¤±è´¥çš„IDåˆ—è¡¨å·²ä¿å­˜åœ¨: ${INFO_FAILED_IDS_FILE}"
    echo "    è„šæœ¬å°†ä»…ä½¿ç”¨å·²æˆåŠŸçš„ ${FINAL_SUCCESS_COUNT} ä¸ªè§†é¢‘ç»§ç»­ä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥ã€‚"

</code></pre>
